<p>&lt;div id=&quot;eaembedcodecontentcustom&quot;&gt;&lt;link rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot; type=&quot;text/css&quot; href=&quot;/resource/INFAKBResource/css/bootstrap-ea.css&quot; onload=&quot;fnDoKBCssRefresh(this);&quot;/&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;.expert-question{color:#0069aa}.collapsing {-webkit-transition: none;transition: none;}&lt;/style&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;container&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;masthead&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;row&quot; style=&quot;padding:10px 20px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-left&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-right&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse in&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Planner for MDM MDE v10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica  Upgrade Planner has been designed and created by the Informatica Global Customer  Support team to provide an insight into the Informatica product upgrades. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;br /&gt;This interactive self-service guide will provide you the information  required to upgrade to Master Data Management (MDM) Multidomain Edition (MDE) v10.0. In this guide, you will learn  about the new features, architectural changes and steps to upgrade. Additionally, it  includes different types of upgrade and best practices to follow during the upgrade cycle.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade process consists of the following phases:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Perform the pre-upgrade tasks&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade Hub store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade Process server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade steps may involve additional steps based on the version you are upgrading from. To start with the upgrade, let us understand your existing implementation.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Note: It is always recommended to run the upgrade on a small copy of production data in the development environment before you upgrade the production.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Please select your existing MDM version...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#e6a613e0-8045-11e4-9f33-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backe6a613e0-8045-11e4-9f33-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;9.6.x&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;4a30ec10-9049-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Types of Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Upgrade steps differ based on the type of upgrade involved.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;The following are the two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;On-Premise&lt;/strong&gt;: This type of upgrade uses the same machine or box by upgrading the OS, application server version or database server version etc., to be compliant with v10.0 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Remote&lt;/strong&gt;:&amp;nbsp;This type of upgrade involves a new machine or box with all the PAM compliant OS, application server or database server etc.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the type of upgrade...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#9d316570-9049-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#4a30ec10-9049-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back9d316570-9049-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#4a30ec10-9049-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Remote&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#922e1560-904e-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Remote Upgrade - New Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Remote upgrade is a brand new installation on new machine with all the supported PAM components.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;If the machine is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;If the machine is a Hub Server or Process Server, then a supported OS and version, application server version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store upgrade has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of AVOS installation, ensure that AVOS schema is created as part of Hub Store installation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the installers for Informatica Platform and AVOS. Refer to PAM for the supported versions.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of Platform installation, configure the platform properties file. Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; or download the sample properties file mentioned in the following KB article:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process server application deployment.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Integrating and/or upgrading external cleanse engines.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Post upgrade tasks such as:  </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Pre-requisites&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Get the MDM license if your implementation involves additional components.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Get the installers from Informatica support by raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Operating System (OS), application server and database server versions as per v10.0 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to the upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#b98a2140-9048-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#895c9e40-8ff7-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backb98a2140-9048-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#895c9e40-8ff7-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#895c9e40-8ff7-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back6f36d240-8045-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#895c9e40-8ff7-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back895c9e40-8ff7-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#895c9e40-8ff7-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#895c9e40-8ff7-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;add84380-9283-11e4-bd2f-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Enable PL/SQL user exits </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Apply CMXUE package&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;For Oracle database, enable user exits by adding the properties to cmxserver.properties file. Please refer&lt;a title=&quot;901Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13048&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more details.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database and application server.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the data using DVT tool -&amp;nbsp;Please refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;901Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13048&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more details&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update references to deprecated features. </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update packages, user exits, views or stored procedures to eliminate references to deprecated objects such as REL_START_DATE, REL_END_DATE, DIRTY_IND and HUID table.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata: </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve the metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable): </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp; </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix 3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.4.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 12, 13, 13.5 and 14&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Integrating and/or upgrading external cleanse engines.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Post upgrade tasks such as:  </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Enable PL/SQL user exits  </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Apply CMXUE package&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;For Oracle database, enable user exits by adding the properties to cmxserver.properties file. Please refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13048&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more details.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database and application server.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the Match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded Metadata:    </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve the metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):    </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;    </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server installation - Platform installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;v10.0 has a tight integration with Informatica Platform, which will allow you to combine the ETL process and MDM Stage process into one Transformation. With this integration, Data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub server. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Before You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading to v10.0, follow these best practices for a smoother upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the Schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Prepare to upgrade to AVOS [Optional]&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve or close all the open tasks managed by Siperian BPM engine if you plan to upgrade to AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Create an AVOS Schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation, please refer &lt;a title=&quot;901Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13048&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt; for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Process Server Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Process server upgrade involves:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process server application deployment.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Integrating and/or upgrading external cleanse engines.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Post upgrade tasks such as:  </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for detailed steps on each of the activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Does your implementation involve any external cleanse engine?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Upgrade - Platform Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.0 has a tight integration with Informatica Platform, which will allow you to combine the ETL process and MDM Stage process into one transformation. With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server upgrade, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub server.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any Platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the Platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.4.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 12, 13, 13.5 and 14&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;ac72a210-8045-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - 9.5.x to v10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.5.x to v10.0, there are major architectural changes. One of the intermediate version had moved the consolidation logic from database tier to application server tier for better performance and supportability of new database (here, SQLServer). Following are the new additions:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.5.x to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Database      agnostic release&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Timeline      granularity&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Change in      Tokenization logic&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Support for Jasper      Reports in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Capability to      have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica      Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Composite object and Composite services&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Entity 360 view&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.5.x to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hard Delete      Detection - now to be enabled in Java user exits&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Changes in post      merge, pre and post unmerge user exits&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;User exit SIF      Framework&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IBM DB2 setup -      disable Oracle-compatibility mode&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Batch unmerge -      moved to Java&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Link style Base objects&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Database user      exits&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF      Framework&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD native      workflow - Replaced with AVOS BPM engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backac72a210-8045-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#ac72a210-8045-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13055&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata: </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable: </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp; </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back3f5a9f70-904e-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3f5a9f70-904e-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3f5a9f70-904e-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;3a10b7b0-9284-11e4-8e42-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Pre-requisites&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store upgrade has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of AVOS installation, ensure that AVOS schema is created as part of Hub Store installation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the installers for Informatica Platform and AVOS. Refer to PAM for the supported versions.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of Platform installation, configure the platform properties file. Refer to the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; or download the sample properties file mentioned in the following KB article:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>

If the machine or box is a Hub Server or Process Server, then upgrade to a supported OS and version, application server version. Once the machine is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.0 has a tighter integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix 3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.4.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 12, 13, 13.5 and 14&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;To upgrade AddressDoctor from earlier versions to 5.4.1, refer the following KB article (steps remains the same even though MDM version pointing in the KB is older):&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/howto/3/Pages/141285.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;HOW TO: Upgrade the version of AddressDoctor from 5.2.5.624 to 5.2.7.785 in MDM 9.1.0 (KB 141285)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to post upgrade/install steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Before You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading to v10.0, follow these best practices for a smoother upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.    </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the Schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade:    </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Store Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hub Store upgrade involves the following:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt; for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub store. Before you upgrade the Hub Store, ensure that database version and OS are v10 PAM compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.0 has a tighter integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;After successfully completing your Hub Store upgrade, lets move on to Hub Server installation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed to the Hub Server upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store      upgrade has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of AVOS      installation, ensure that AVOS schema is created as part of Hub Store      installation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the      installers for Informatica Platform and AVOS. Refer the PAM for supported      versions.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of platform installation, configure the platform properties file. (KB      306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Server upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#34fabe40-8c14-11e4-a247-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;53b21880-927f-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Enable PL/SQL user exits </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Apply CMXUE package&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;For Oracle database, enable user exits by adding the properties to cmxserver.properties file. Please refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13048&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more details.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database and application server.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update references to deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the Match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata.   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve the metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the AVOS (if applicable):   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>

(KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? <p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to Hub Server post installation tasks?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - From 9.6.x to v10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.6.x to v10.0, there are no major architectural changes. Version 9.6 being a database agnostic release, it only supports SQLServer database. Later release such as 9.6.1 and 9.6.1 HotFix 1, supports other databases also (Oracle and DB2). Following are the new additions:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.6.x to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Proximity search&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Data encryption&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Language selection in Hub console&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Capability to have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;ActiveVOS Integration&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Composite object and Composite services&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Entity 360 view&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.6.x to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Default Proxy role&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;SIF - EJB2 Protocols&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF Framework&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD native workflow - Replaced with AVOS BPM engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process server application deployment.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Integrating external cleanse engines.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Post installation tasks such as:  </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; Point to the existing MDM installation folder while running the installer to upgrade Hub Server on to v10.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Also, MDM v10.0 has a tight integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. IDD native workflow is replaced by the ActiveVOS BPM capabilities.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;if you do not want to install ActiveVOS as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;There are two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Pre-requisites&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store installation has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of AVOS installation, ensure that AVOS schema is created as part of Hub Store installation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the installers for Informatica Platform and AVOS. Refer &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/community/my-support/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; for the supported versions.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of Platform installation, configure the platform properties file. Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; or download the sample properties file mentioned in the following KB article:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Server installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#eaae2080-89ba-11e4-a247-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#13b8f100-89b9-11e4-8ef6-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backeaae2080-89ba-11e4-a247-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#13b8f100-89b9-11e4-8ef6-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13055&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata: </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable: </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp; </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back1c97e0d0-8c2d-11e4-a5f4-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#1c97e0d0-8c2d-11e4-a5f4-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#1c97e0d0-8c2d-11e4-a5f4-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;d2bef910-904d-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Process Server Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Process server installation involves the following:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process server application deployment&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Integrating external cleanse engines&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Post installation tasks such as:  </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for detailed steps on each of the activity.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Does your implementation involve any external cleanse engine?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;li&gt;Get the MDM license if your implementation involves additional components.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Get the installers from Informatica support by raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Operating System (OS), Application server and Database server versions as per v10.0 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to the upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Types of Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Upgrade steps differ based on the type of upgrade involved.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;There are two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;On-Premise&lt;/strong&gt;: This type of upgrade uses the same machine or box by upgrading the Operating System (OS), application server version or database server version etc., to be compliant with v10.0 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Remote:&lt;/strong&gt; This type of upgrade involves a new machine or box with all the PAM compliant OS, application server or database server etc.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the type of upgrade...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a144d420-8c12-11e4-a5f4-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#12515170-8047-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa144d420-8c12-11e4-a5f4-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#12515170-8047-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;On-Premise&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#1c6d6ce0-89a5-11e4-a5f4-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#12515170-8047-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back1c6d6ce0-89a5-11e4-a5f4-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#12515170-8047-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Remote&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back12515170-8047-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#12515170-8047-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#12515170-8047-11e4-8db8-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;922e1560-904e-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;On-Premise Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;On-premise upgrade is upgrading all the components of existing host machine, components such as Operating system, JDK, Application server version, Database version etc.,If the box is for Hub store, then we need to upgrade to a supported Operating System, Database version. If the box is a Hub server or Process server, then we need to upgrade to a supported Operating System and version, Application server version.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Once the box is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica MySupport portal&lt;/a&gt;. Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that the database version and OS are v10 PAM compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.0 has a tighter integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema, which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the 'Create an Informatica AVOS Schema' section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.      </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.      </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.4.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 12, 13, 13.5 and 14&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;To upgrade AddressDoctor from earlier versions to 5.4.1, refer the following KB article (steps remains the same even though MDM version pointing in the KB is older):&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/howto/3/Pages/141285.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;HOW TO: Upgrade the version of AddressDoctor from 5.2.5.624 to 5.2.7.785 in MDM 9.1.0 (KB 141285)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to post upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back041adda0-9286-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#041adda0-9286-11e4-a579-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; Point to the existing MDM installation folder while running the installer to upgrade Hub Server on to v10.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Also, MDM v10.0 has a tight integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. IDD native workflow is replaced by the ActiveVOS BPM capabilities.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;if you do not want to install ActiveVOS as part of Hub server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt; for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. Before you upgrade the Hub Store, ensure that database version and OS are v10 PAM compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.0 has a tighter integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;if you do not want to install ActiveVOS as part of Hub server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to &lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13055&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt; for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:          </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable:          </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;          </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back99b4ceb0-89ef-11e4-a247-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#99b4ceb0-89ef-11e4-a247-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#4a4fc230-8044-11e4-91a3-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#99b4ceb0-89ef-11e4-a247-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;beb03340-8c23-11e4-a247-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Upgrade - Post Installation Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Post upgrade tasks of Hub Server involves:&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Manually deploying Hub Server application for application      clusters&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Manually      creating data sources&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Manually      creating JMS queues&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Repackaging      custom jar files&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;JBoss cache      configuration&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for clear instructions on every task mentioned above.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - 9.7.x to v10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.7.x to v10.0, there are no major architectural changes. One optional feature of integrating Platform to MDM is the key highlights of this release. Following are the new additions:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.7.x to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Language selection in Hub console&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Capability to have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Composite object and Composite services&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Entity 360 view&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.5.x to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Default Proxy role&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;SIF - EJB2 Protocols&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF Framework&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD native workflow - Replaced with AVOS BPM engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; IDD native workflow is replaced by the ActiveVOS BPM capabilities.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Operating System (OS), application server and database server versions as per v10.0 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to the upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.       </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup the Schema - Database Backup&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup Customizations such as User Exit code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.        </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Generate the Readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the Upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot;
