for detailed steps on each of the activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Does your implementation involve any external cleanse engine?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Remote Upgrade - New Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Remote upgrade is a brand new installation on new machine with all the supported PAM components.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is a Hub Server or Process Server, then a supported OS and version, application server version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine or box is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server upgrade, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13055&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata: </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable: </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp; </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is a Hub Server or Process Server, then a supported OS and version, application server version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine or box is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store installation has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of AVOS installation, ensure that AVOS schema is created as part of Hub Store installation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the installers for Informatica Platform and AVOS. Refer &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/community/my-support/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; for the supported versions.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Incase of Platform installation, configure the platform properties file. Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; or download the sample properties file mentioned in the following KB article:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/infakb/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.4.1&lt;/li&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt; for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. Before you upgrade the Hub Store, ensure that database version and OS are v10 PAM compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.0 has a tighter integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;After successfully completing your Hub Store upgrade, lets move on to Hub Server installation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed to the Hub Server installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; Point to the existing MDM installation folder while running the installer to upgrade Hub Server on to v10.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Also, MDM v10.0 has a tight integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. IDD native workflow is replaced by the ActiveVOS BPM capabilities.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;if you do not want to install ActiveVOS as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/product-documents.jspa?containerType=14&amp;amp;containerID=2333&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;No&lt;/em&gt; if you do not want to install ActiveVOS as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to proceed with the Hub Server installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;There are two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ol&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;On-Premise&lt;/strong&gt;: This type of upgrade uses the same machine or box by upgrading the OS, application server version or database server version etc. to be compliant with v10.0 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Remote&lt;/strong&gt;:&amp;nbsp;This type of upgrade involves a new machine or box with all the PAM compliant OS, application server or database server etc.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the type of upgrade...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.0, there are major architectural changes. One of the intermediate version has moved the consolidation logic from database tier to application server tier for better performance and supportability of new database (here, SQLServer). Following are the new additions:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Timeline &lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Database      agnostic release&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Change in      Tokenization logic&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Support for Jasper      Reports in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Capability to      have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Informatica      Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Composite object and Composite services&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Entity 360 view&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Foreign Key      merge lineage is maintained in XREF table&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Merge lineage is      maintained in XREF table&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;HM Relationship      effective dates are replaced by Period_Start_Date and Period_End_Date&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hard Delete      Detection - now to be enabled in Java user exits&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Changes in post      merge, pre and post unmerge user exits&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;User exit SIF      Framework&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IBM DB2 setup -      disable Oracle-compatibility mode&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Batch unmerge -      moved to Java&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Link style Base objects&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Database user      exits&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF      Framework&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD native      workflow - Replaced with AVOS BPM engine&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>

<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Enable PL/SQL user exits</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Apply CMXUE package&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;For Oracle database, enable user exits by adding the properties to cmxserver.properties file. Please refer &lt;a title=&quot;901Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13048&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt; for more details.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database and application server.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the data using DVT tool -&amp;nbsp;Please refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;901Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/docs/DOC-13048&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more details&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update references to deprecated features.</p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Update packages, user exits, views or stored procedures to eliminate references to deprecated objects such as REL_START_DATE, REL_END_DATE, DIRTY_IND and HUID table.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Resolve the metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Implement updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </p>
<p>&lt;ul&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
